                        <div data-reactid="302">
                         2 large bedroom suite sleeps 4 one queen size bed and one regular size bed. Private bathroom in between rooms. This space is your home away from home.

                        <div data-reactid="303">
                         Private bedroom and bath on lake with screened in porch, offer peaceful nights. Cook or grill out and enjoy your meals on our private patio. Located near golf/soccer course, 30 minutes to Discovery Park/Reelfoot Lake, 20 minutes from Sloonshine Distillery, 84.4 miles from Graceland, walking distance to coffee shop, restaurants, workout gym. Our home is located on a beautiful peaceful pond in town. You can paddle around, roast marshmallows, sit by a fire or just chill and watch the sunset. We are located on a nice golf course, soccer golf course and pool which are additional cost according to the Country Club rates. If grilling out is something you enjoy we have a charcoal grill. We are one mile from a lovely park and walking distance to Java Cafe, El Patio, Abe's Ribeye Barn, a 24/7 fitness gym, yogurt and donut shop. You are welcome to fish in the pond but please bring a fishing pole. There is a bait shop within walking distance as well. There is nothing better than stretching out and taking a nap on the 6 ft wicker swing or reading a book it's just wonderful. If you get a chance The Discovery Museum is a short 30 minute drive and so is Reelfoot Lake. These places are great day trips! Graceland and Beale Street are 83 miles from our driveway, so it's a easy day trip as well. If hunting is your pleasure we have lots of land good for duck, turkey and deer hunting for a additional fee. I also have a baby bed and a tanning bed if you want to take advantage of them you are more than welcome. Feel free to use the kitchen, dining areas, patios, grills, bike, boats, refrigerator, TV's and music. There is a sunroom with TV's and cable /Netflix . We also have free WI-FI. We will probably be here when you are but we won't bother you unless you need us. If you want interaction we will be glad to visit but while you are here at The Shack on the Pond we want you to be our guest and relax. You will be staying in a very friendly and safe neighborhood, so walking or biking at night is no problem. It's also close to everything. You can walk right up the street and get coffee, Chinese food, Mexican food, donuts, yogurt, a great steak, your nails done, workout and more. Your car, walking or my bike are the best ways to get around. We are excited and welcome you to our home. We will do everything possible to make your stay pleasant, fun, memorable and relaxing.

                      <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="1230">
                       <div data-reactid="1231">
                        <div data-reactid="1232">
                         Find your piece of paradise at the Carver Lake Lodge in Perryville, MO. Our property consists of 85 acres with use of our own private 17 acre lake. The Cash Lodge can sleep up to 6 people. Master w/ queen bed, second bedroom with bunk beds, and a sofa sleeper in the family room. Has lake views on the huge deck and a full kitchen with stainless appliances. Close to Castor River, state parks, Taum Sauk, Johnson's Shut-Ins, Millstream Gardens, Pickle Springs, Elephant Rocks, and many wineries.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1233">
                         The Cash Lodge is a 2 bedroom, 1 bath ranch-style lodge that sleeps up to 6 people, 4 adults and 2 children comfortably. Note that the daily rent includes four guests; additional guests are $10 per guest per night. It is completely updated with new central air and heat and offers 720 square feet of cozy country living. Besides the queen bed in the master and the bunk bed in the kids bedroom, there is also a queen-sized sofa sleeper in the family room with an upgraded memory foam mattress. There is a tub and shower combo in the bathroom and stainless steel appliances consisting of a refrigerator, glass top electric range, over the range microwave, and a dishwasher for your cooking needs. Brand new sliding glass doors lead to a stately 360 square foot deck with unbelievable views of the lake and ridge, and plenty of outdoor deck seating to hang out for hours.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1234">
                         We are about a 20 minute drive from the Perryville exit (Exit 129) on Highway 55. We are far enough from the city to have your own privacy and close enough to make a run to Walmart or restaurants for a quick meal or supply run. Besides enjoying the 85 acre paradise with your private 17 acre stocked lake, there is a lot to do near Perryville. We are close to historic Sainte Genevieve, Hahn State Park for hiking, and 45 minutes from Cape Girardeau. There are also many wineries within a 30-60 minute drive from the farm.
                        </div>

                        <div data-reactid="1363">
                         Private bedroom with Jack and Jill private bath. Pond view with 4 patios. Separate work area right down the hall with desk, refrigerator, sofa, books and games for work or play. Internet access inside and outside. Perfect for business or relaxing. Ironing board and iron also available for convenience.

                        <div data-reactid="1364">
                         Private bedroom and bath on lake with screened in porch, offer peaceful nights. Cook or grill out and enjoy your meals on our private patio. Located near golf/soccer course, 30 minutes to Discovery Park/Reelfoot Lake, 20 minutes from Sloonshine Distillery, 84.4 miles from Graceland, walking distance to coffee shop, restaurants, workout gym. Our home is located on a beautiful peaceful pond right in the best part of town. You can paddle around, roast marshmallows, sit by a fire or just chill and watch the sunset. We are located close to a nice golf course, and pool which are additional cost according to the clubhouse rates. FOR BUSINESS TRAVELERS ONLY, if you need a catered meal or dinner while staying here I am a cater and would be happy to help you plan your next lunch or dinner here at our home for a additional fee. We have a private dining room that will accommodate 10-12 adults. If grilling out is something you enjoy we have a charcoal grill. We are one mile from a lovely park and walking distance to Java Cafe, El Patio, Abe's Ribeye Barn, a 24/7 fitness gym, yogurt and donut shop. You are welcome to fish in the pond but please bring a fishing pole. There is a bait shop within walking distance as well. There is nothing better than stretching out and taking a nap on the 6 ft wicker swing or reading a book it's just wonderful. If you get a chance The Discovery Museum is a short 30 minute drive and so is Reelfoot Lake. These places are great day trips! Graceland and Beale Street are 83 miles from our driveway, so it's a easy day trip as well. If hunting is your pleasure we have lots of land good for duck, turkey and deer hunting for a additional fee. Feel free to use the kitchen, dining areas, patios, grills, bike, boats, refrigerator, TV's and music. There is a sunroom with TV's and cable /Netflix . We also have free WI-FI. We will probably be here when you are but we won't bother you unless you need us. If you want interaction we will be glad to visit but while you are here at The Shack on the Pond we want you to be our guest and relax. You will be staying in a very friendly and safe neighborhood, so walking or biking at night is no problem. It's also close to everything. You can walk right up the street and get coffee, Chinese food, Mexican food, donuts, yogurt, a great steak, your nails done, workout and more. Your car, walking or my bike are the best ways to get around.

                        <div data-reactid="2212">
                         Located on the second floor of a Victorian home built in 1890, this private room has a queen bed and a small sitting area. You will have a private entrance off of a cozy side porch. There is also a full bath and kitchenette, both of which are shared with the other bedroom. Second bedroom available to rent.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="2213">
                         Great space in the quiet Lowertown Arts District Neighborhood. This large bedroom has a queen bed and sitting area that make the room cozy. There is a kitchenette with coffee maker, toaster, microwave and refrigerator. Dishes and silverware are also provided. Fresh, locally roasted coffee from Righteous Roast Coffee Company(the homeowner), is provided for you to brew each day. Secluded side porch offers you privacy, and is great for sitting and enjoying your morning coffee or afternoon cocktail. A total of two bedrooms are available on the second floor of this home. Both bedrooms have a sitting area. If both bedrooms are booked by the same party, the entire second floor is available for use. The cost for entire second floor is $125/ night. If separate parties book the two bedrooms, then the bathroom and kitchenette are shared. The bedrooms and bathroom lock for security.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="2214">
                         The home is located in the Lowertown Arts District Neighborhood. You will only be a few blocks from the Ohio River and Downtown Paducah where there are family owned restaurants, shopping, museums, Yeiser Art Center, the Carson Four Rivers Performing Arts Center, Market House Theatre and Maiden Alley Cinema, the region’s only Independent Film ArtHouse. The National Quilt Museum is only four blocks from us.
